		<div id="ld-fancy-heading-69a6c1a40ff73" class="ld-fancy-heading pos-rel">
			<h2 class="ld-fh-element d-inline-block pos-rel  elementor-heading-title lqd-highlight-classic lqd-highlight-grow-left h2"  data-inview="true" data-transition-delay="true" data-delay-options="{&quot;elements&quot;:&quot;.lqd-highlight-inner&quot;,&quot;delayType&quot;:&quot;transition&quot;}" > <span class="lqd-adv-txt-item elementor-repeater-item-a2474c6">Hello!</span></h2>		</div>

				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-c2b7518 elementor-widget elementor-widget-hub_fancy_heading" data-id="c2b7518" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="hub_fancy_heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					
		<div id="ld-fancy-heading-69a6c1a4104a0" class="ld-fancy-heading pos-rel">
			<p class="ld-fh-element d-inline-block pos-rel  lqd-highlight-classic lqd-highlight-grow-left p"  > I’m Khyati Thaker, a lawyer-turned-travel planner who swapped legal briefs for boarding passes. After nearly a decade of structured work in the legal world, I now apply the same analytical, detail-driven thinking to international travel planning.

At A Lawyer’s Voyage (ALV), I help first-time and occasional international travellers plan smarter trips — saving time, money, and unnecessary stress. 

My work focuses on thoughtful routing, realistic pacing, and better decisions before booking, whether through travel plan reviews or ready-made itineraries.

With a strong focus on Europe and Asia, every trip — from popular routes to quietly special experiences — is planned with intention, not overwhelm

Because good travel planning isn’t about doing more.
It’s about doing it right.</p>		</div>
